### Turn 5 · 20 Mar 2026 14:45 IST

**Student asked:**

> Say me which easy nata or jee main paper 2 exam

**Aintra answered:**

> That's a very common question students ask! It's not straightforward to say one is definitively "easier" than the other, as they test different skill sets and knowledge areas. However, we can highlight their core differences:
> 
> **NATA (National Aptitude Test in Architecture):**
> *   **Focus:** Primarily assesses your aptitude for architecture, drawing skills, aesthetic sensitivity, visual perception, and general awareness.
> *   **Maths & Physics:** Covers basic concepts from the 10+2 level. The emphasis is more on foundational understanding rather than complex problem-solving.
> *   **Drawing:** Tests creativity, observation, and ability to sketch and represent ideas.
> *   **Overall:** Many students find NATA to be more aptitude-based and less dependent on advanced science and math knowledge compared to JEE Main Paper 2. If you have strong drawing skills and a good general aptitude, you might find NATA more approachable.
> 
> **JEE Main Paper 2 (for B.Arch/B.Planning):**
> *   **Focus:** Has a stronger academic emphasis, particularly on Mathematics.
> *   **Maths:** The Mathematics section is generally considered more challenging, similar in depth to the JEE Main Paper 1 (for B.Tech) level, requiring a solid grasp of 11th and 12th-grade concepts.
> *   **Aptitude:** Similar to NATA, it tests general aptitude.
> *   **Drawing:** While it also has a drawing section, it often leans more towards technical drawing, 3D perception, and perspective rather than purely aesthetic or creative drawing.
> *   **Overall:** JEE Main Paper 2 is often perceived as more academically rigorous, especially due to its Mathematics section. If you excel in advanced math and physics, you might find JEE Paper 2 aligns better with your strengths.
> 
> **In summary:**
> If your strengths lie in **drawing, creativity, and general aptitude**, NATA might feel "easier" or more aligned with your skills.
> If you have a **strong command over 11th and 12th-grade Mathematics and Physics** and enjoy more technical problem-solving, JEE Main Paper 2 might be where you shine.
> 
> At Neram Classes, we offer coaching for both NATA and JEE Paper 2 because many students prepare for both to maximize their chances of getting into a top B.Arch/B.Planning program.
> 
> Do you have a preference for one over the other, or are you considering preparing for both?

_model: gemini-2.5-flash · 4951 ms_

This includes most private architecture colleges, many state government-funded colleges, and various universities offering B.Arch programs. If a college offers a B.Arch degree, there's a very high chance they will accept NATA scores as a primary eligibility criterion.

**Aintra answered:**

> 
> Generally, **IIITs (Indian Institutes of Information Technology) primarily focus on Information Technology, Computer Science, and related engineering disciplines.** They are not typically known for offering Bachelor of Architecture (B.Arch) programs.
> 
> B.Arch programs are usually offered by institutions like:
> *   **NITs (National Institutes of Technology)**
> *   **SPAs (Schools of Planning and Architecture)**
> *   Various **state government and private universities**
> *   **Deemed universities**
> 
> So, if you're looking to pursue a B.Arch degree, you would typically aim for these types of institutions rather than IIITs.

**Student asked:**

> For anna University I need the nata score only not the jee main paper 2 marks

**Aintra answered:**

> That's correct! For B.Arch admissions in colleges affiliated with **Anna University** (and most other state government and private colleges in Tamil Nadu), your **NATA score** is the primary entrance examination considered.
> 
> **JEE Main Paper 2 marks are generally NOT used for admission to Anna University affiliated B.Arch programs.**
> 
> The admission process typically involves:
> 1.  Having a valid **NATA score**.
> 2.  Your 10+2 (or equivalent) academic marks.
> 3.  Participating in the **TNEA B.Arch counselling** conducted by the Directorate of Technical Education (DoTE) Tamil Nadu, where your NATA score and academic performance will be combined to determine your rank for seat allocation.
> 
> So, yes, focus on your NATA score for Anna University!
>

**Aintra answered:**

> Yes, absolutely! You can appear for NATA 2026 while you are in your 11th grade. The official NATA 2026 eligibility criteria states that you must be "Passed or appearing in 10+2 with subjects specified by CoA" to appear for the exam. Since you are in 11th grade, you are considered to be "appearing" for your 10+2 examinations in the future.
> 
> However, please keep in mind that to be eligible for B.Arch admission after NATA, you will need to successfully pass your 10+2 (12th grade) with Physics, Mathematics (compulsory), and one of Chemistry, Biology, Technical Vocational, CS, IT, Informatics Practices, Engineering Graphics, or Business Studies, with a minimum aggregate of 45%.
> 
> Your NATA 2026 score will be valid for the academic session 2026-2027 only. This means if you take NATA this year, you can use the score for admissions in 2026, provided you meet the 10+2 criteria by then. This is a great opportunity to get a head start on your preparation and experience the exam.

_model: gemini-2.5-flash · 2224 ms_  

### Turn 2 · 05 Mar 2026 13:15 IST

**Student asked:**

> nata eligibility score ?

**Aintra answered:**

> To qualify the NATA exam, you need to achieve a specific minimum score. These are the NATA eligibility scores set by the Council of Architecture (COA) for the NATA 2026 exam:
> 
> *   **Part A (Drawing):** Minimum 20 marks out of 80
> *   **Part B (MCQ + Aptitude):** Minimum 20 marks out of 120
> *   **Overall NATA Score:** Minimum 60 marks out of 200
> 
> It's important to note that you must meet all three criteria to be considered "NATA qualified." If you take multiple attempts, the best score from all your attempts will be considered for your final NATA score.
> 
> While 60 marks is the qualifying score, aiming for a much higher score will significantly improve your chances of getting admission to a top B.Arch college. Neram Classes offers comprehensive coaching and mock tests to help you achieve your best possible score!
